 The two Indian Army officers, currently deployed as peacekeepers in South Sudan, are part of the contingent that will ascend Kilimanjaro, Africa's highest peak, to spread the message of maintaining peace and stability in the continent
 tippaniyan The team led by Colonel Dipinder Virk consists of Major Vikas Kumar and Romania's Major Liviu Chande
 dal ke christmas ke din 19,340 foot kii is chotii ko fatah karne kii ummid he
 According to the information provided by the world body and the mission based in South Sudan, the three people will hoist the United Nations flag and broadcast the message of peace, reaching the highest peak of the continent
 virk ne kaha ki unki yah yatra africa or mukhya taur par dakshini sudan main shanti or sthirataa laane ke sanyukt raashtra ke prayaason kii pratik he
 He said, "we do not think of borders, we are here for the peace of the continent
" yadi dakshini sudan main shanti aati he to yah saare africa ke nivaasiyon ke prayaas se aani chahie
 '' karnal dipinder virk ke netritv vaali team main major vikaas kumaar or romania ke major liviyu chende hai
 The party is expected to conquer this 19,340-foot peak on Christmas day
 vishwa nikaay or dakshini sudan sthit mishan dwaara muhaiyaa karai gai jaankaree ke anusaar is mahadweep kii sabase oonchi chotii par pahunchakar teenon log sanyukt raashtra kaa jhanda fahraayenge or shanti ke sandesh ko prasaarit karenge
